That duty instead came from somewhere else, and the weight of authority indicates that it came from a business's act of holding itself out to the public as ready to serve anyone who would hire it.  Singer 1304-1330; 3 W. Blackstone, Commentaries on the Laws of England 164 (1768); J. Story, Commentaries on the Law of Bailments 495, 591 (1837); 1 T. Parsons, Law of Contracts 639, 643, 649 (1853).</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 7" name="FNopinion1.7" href="#FRopinion1.7">7</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;Compare, <em>e.g.</em>, <em>Chesapeake, O. &amp; S. R. Co.</em> v. <em>Wells</em>, 85 Tenn. 613, 615, 4 S. W. 5 (1887) (rejecting Ida B. Wells's claim that she was denied "&nbsp;'accommodations equal in all respects,'&nbsp;" when she tried to enter a train car "set apart for white ladies and their gentlemen" on account of tobacco smoke in her car, and was forcibly removed), with <em>Memphis &amp; C. R. Co.</em> v. <em>Benson</em>, 85 Tenn. 627, 632, 4 S. W. 5, 7 (1887) (accepting that a white man would be permitted to ride standing in the ladies' car on account of tobacco smoke in his car).</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 8" name="FNopinion1.8" href="#FRopinion1.8">8</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;See Cal. Civ. Code Ann. 51; Colo. Rev. Stat. 24-34-601; Conn. Gen. Stat. 46a-81d; Del. Code Ann., Tit. 6, 4504; Haw. Rev. Stat. 489-3; Ill. Comp. Stat., ch. 775, 5/1-102; Iowa Code 216.7; Me. Rev. Stat. Ann., Tit. 5, 4591; Md. State Govt. Code Ann. 20-304; Mass. Gen. Laws, ch. 272, 98; Mich. Comp. Laws 37.2302, as amended; Minn. Stat. 363A.11; Nev. Rev. Stat. 651.070; N.&nbsp;H. Rev. Stat. Ann. 354-A:17; N.&nbsp;J. Stat. Ann. 10:5-12; N.&nbsp;M. Stat. Ann. 28-1-7; N.&nbsp;Y. Civ. Rights Law Ann. 40; Ore. Rev. Stat. 659A.403; R.&nbsp;I. Gen. Laws 11-24-2; Vt. Stat. Ann., Tit. 9, 4502; Va. Code Ann. 2.2-3904; Wash. Rev. Code 49.60.215; Wis. Stat. 106.52.</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 9" name="FNopinion1.9" href="#FRopinion1.9">9</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;The majority commits a fundamental error in suggesting that a law does not regulate conduct if it ever applies to expressive activities.  See <em>ante</em>, at 19, 22.  This would come as a great surprise to the <em>O'Brien</em> Court.</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 10" name="FNopinion1.10" href="#FRopinion1.10">10</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;The majority appears to find this discussion of the Communication Clause upsetting.  See <em>ante</em>, at 20-21, and n.&nbsp;5.  It is easy to understand why: The Court's prior First Amendment cases clearly explain that a ban on discrimination may require a business to take down a sign that expresses the business owner's intent to discriminate.  See, <em>e.g.</em>, <em>FAIR</em>, 547 U.&nbsp;S., at 62.  This principle is deeply inconsistent with the majority's position.  Thus, a "straight couples only" notice, like the one the Court today allows, see App. to Pet. for Cert. 188a-189a, is itself a devastating indictment of the majority's logic.</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 11" name="FNopinion1.11" href="#FRopinion1.11">11</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;Because petitioners have never sold a wedding website to anyone, the record contains only a mockup website.  The mockup confirms what you would expect: The website provides details of the event, a form to RSVP, a gift registry, etc.  See App. 51-72.  The customization of these elements pursuant to a content-neutral regulation of conduct does not unconstitutionally intrude upon any protected expression of the website designer.  Yet Smith claims a First Amendment right to refuse to provide <em>any</em> wedding website for a same-sex couple.  Her claim therefore rests on the idea that her act of service is itself a form of protected expression.  In granting Smith's claim, the majority collapses the distinction between status-based and message-based refusals of service.  The history shows just how profoundly wrong that is.  See <em>Runyon</em> v. <em>McCrary</em>, 427 U.&nbsp;S. 160, 176 (1976); <em>Hishon</em> v. <em>King &amp; Spalding</em>, 467 U.&nbsp;S. 69, 78 (1984);<em> Roberts</em> v. <em>United States Jaycees</em>, 468 U.&nbsp;S. 609, 622-629 (1984).</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 12" name="FNopinion1.12" href="#FRopinion1.12">12</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;The majority tacitly acknowledges the absurdity.  At the start of its opinion, it explains that Smith "decided to expand her offerings to include services for couples seeking websites for <em>their</em> weddings."  <em>Ante</em>, at&nbsp;1 (emphasis added).</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 13" name="FNopinion1.13" href="#FRopinion1.13">13</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;What is "&nbsp;'embarrassing'&nbsp;" about this reasoning is not, as the Court claims, the "distinction between status and message."  <em>Ante</em>, at 18, n.&nbsp;3.  It is petitioners' contrivance, embraced by the Court, that a prohibition on status-based discrimination can be avoided by asserting that a group can always buy services on behalf of others, or else that the group can access a "separate but equal" subset of the services made available to everyone else.</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 14" name="FNopinion1.14" href="#FRopinion1.14">14</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;The majority's repeated invocation of this Orwellian thought policing is revealing of just how much it misunderstands this case.  See <em>ante</em>, at 10-12, 19-20, 24-25 (claiming that the State seeks to "eliminate ideas" and that it will punish Smith unless she "conforms her views to the State's").</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 15" name="FNopinion1.15" href="#FRopinion1.15">15</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;These laws variously censor discussion of sexual orientation and  gender identity in schools, see, <em>e.g.</em>, 2023 Ky. Acts pp. 775-779, and ban drag shows in public, see 2023 Tenn. Pub. Acts ch. 2.  Yet we are told that the real threat to free speech is that a commercial business open to the public might have to serve all members of the public.</p>

<br><strong>Footnote <a aria-label="Move to citation 16" name="FNopinion1.16" href="#FRopinion1.16">16</a></strong><br><p>&nbsp;The potential implications of the Court's logic are deeply troubling.  Would <em>Runyon </em>v. <em>McCrary</em> have come out differently if the schools had argued that accepting Black children would have required them to create original speech, like lessons, report cards, or diplomas, that they deeply objected to?  What if the law firm in <em>Hishon </em>v. <em>King &amp; Spalding</em> had argued that promoting a woman to the partnership would have required it to alter its speech, like letterhead or court filings, in ways that it would rather not?  Once you look closely, "compelled speech" (in the majority's facile understanding of that concept) is everywhere.</p>
 
        <p></p>
        <p></p>

        <h2 class="case-information__title"> <span style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: UPPERCASE;"><small>303 CREATIVE LLC ET AL.</small></span> <em>v</em>. <span style="TEXT-TRANSFORM: UPPERCASE;"><small>ELENIS ET AL.</small></span> (2023)</h2>
        
        <p class="case-information__paragraph"><b class="case-information__paragraph-topic">Docket No:</b> No. 21-476</p>
        
        
        <p class="case-information__paragraph"><b class="case-information__paragraph-topic">Argued:</b> December 05, 2022</p>
        <p class="case-information__paragraph"><b class="case-information__paragraph-topic">Decided:</b> June 30, 2023</p>
        <p class="case-information__paragraph"><b class="case-information__paragraph-topic">Court:</b> United States Supreme Court</p>

_satellite.ads.adInfoFactory = function(nameString, href) {
  // TODO remove this once the correct PA is being used for the lid
  if( _satellite.getVar('ad_decision_context') && _satellite.getVar('ad_decision_context').pa ) {
    nameString = nameString.replace(/pa:[0-9]+/, "pa:"+_satellite.getVar('ad_decision_context').pa);  
  }
  _satellite.logger.debug('_satellite.ads.adInfoFactory nameString: '+nameString);

  // sample name: "&lid=clk:fs/prod:dts/cid:5088127/msa:259/pa:1313/sub:3107462/pos:1"
  var s = nameString;
  s = s.substr(5);
  var lid = s;
  s = s.replaceAll(':','":"');
  s = s.replaceAll('/','","');
  s = '{"'+s+'"}'
  var adInfo = JSON.parse(s);
  adInfo.lid = lid;
  adInfo.paid = (typeof adInfo.sub != 'undefined');
  adInfo.adId = (adInfo.paid ? adInfo.sub : adInfo.cid);
  var map = {
    'ph':'phone',
    'fs':'website',
    'pv':'profile',
    'cu':'contact',
    'vr':'review-read',
    'wr':'review-write',
    'sl':'super-lawyers'
  };  
  adInfo.type = map[adInfo.clk];   
  adInfo.transactionId = _satellite.getVar('fl_user_id')+'-'+adInfo.adId+'-'+(new Date().getTime());
  
  if( href && adInfo.type == 'phone' ) {
    adInfo.detail = href.replace(/[^\d]/g,'');
    if( adInfo.detail.length > 10 ) {
      adInfo.detail = adInfo.detail.substr(adInfo.detail.length-10);
    }
  }  
  
  return adInfo;
}

_satellite.ads.trackAdEngagement = function(adInfo) {
  if( typeof adInfo.adId == 'undefined' ) {
    return false;
  }
  if( typeof FLDataLayer.ads == 'undefined' ) {
    FLDataLayer.ads = {};
  }
  if( typeof FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements == 'undefined' ) {
    FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements = [];
  }
  for( var i=0; i < FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements.length; i++ ) {
    if( FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements[i].type == adInfo.type && FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements[i].adId == adInfo.adId ) {
      return true;
    }
  }

  FLDataLayer.ads.adEngagements.push(adInfo);
  return false;
}

  }

function setTrackerCookie(name, value)
{
  var hostParts = location.host.split('.').reverse();
  var cookieDomain = '.' + hostParts[1] + '.' + hostParts[0];
  document.cookie = name + '=' + value + ';domain=' + cookieDomain + ';path=/';
}

window.addEventListener("load", function(event) {
  try {

    _satellite.trackSearchSource = function(type){
      let toStore = type;
      if(type.indexOf("Top-Nav")>-1 || type.indexOf("Next Steps")>-1 ){
        const pageType = _satellite.getVar("page_page_type");
        if(pageType == "article") toStore += " Article";
        if(pageType == "index") toStore += " Index";
      }
      var practiceCode = _satellite.getVar("practice_code");
      if (practiceCode) {
        toStore+= "|"+practiceCode;
      }
      _satellite.logger.info('s_dsource',toStore);
      _satellite.writeCrossSubdomainCookie("s_dsource", toStore);
    };

    _satellite.slowDown = function(e, goTo){
      e.preventDefault(); // prevent default anchor behavior
      setTimeout(function() {
        window.location = goTo;
      }, 300);
    }
    
    //CTA Search - enter & click
    const nextStepsForm = document.querySelector('.nextSteps form');
    _satellite.logger.info('nextStepsForm',nextStepsForm);
    if (nextStepsForm) {
          nextStepsForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
          _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Next Steps");
        });
    }


    //Top Nav & Find a Lawyer Page - Enter
    const searchComponents = document.querySelectorAll('#search-component,.hero-content form, .search-secondary form');
    _satellite.logger.info('searchComponents',searchComponents);
    searchComponents.forEach((component) => {
      component.addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') {
          if (location.host + location.pathname == "lawyers.findlaw.com/") {
            _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Find a Lawyer");
            _satellite.logger.info('Search Box','Find a Lawyer');
          } else {
              _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Top-Nav");
              _satellite.logger.info('Search Box','Top-Nav');
          }
        }
      });
    })
    

    //Top Nav & Find a Lawyer Page - click
    const submitButtons = document.querySelectorAll('submit-button, .hero-content input[type="submit"], .search-secondary input[type="submit"]')
    submitButtons.forEach((button) => {
      _satellite.logger.info('button',button);
      button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (location.host + location.pathname === "lawyers.findlaw.com/") {
          _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Find a Lawyer");
          _satellite.logger.info('Search Box','Find a Lawyer');
        } else {
          _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Top-Nav");
          _satellite.logger.info('Search Box','Top-Nav');
        }
      });
    })

    //Homepage search
    if (location.host + location.pathname === "www.findlaw.com/") {

      _satellite.logger.info('forms',forms);
      forms.forEach((form) => {
        _satellite.logger.info('form',form);
        form.addEventListener('submit', function() {
          _satellite.trackSearchSource("Search Box: Home");
          _satellite.logger.info('Search Box','Home');
        });
      });
    }

    //CTA
    const links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="fli="], .articleHeading p a[href*="lawyers.findlaw.com"]');
    _satellite.logger.info('links',links);
    links.forEach((link) => {
      link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        const goTo = link.getAttribute('href');
        _satellite.slowDown(e, goTo);
        let source = link.dataset.searchLocation || '';
        if (!source) {
          if (link.closest('.cta-public')) {
            source = 'CTA: Banner';
          } else {
            source = 'CTA: Inline Link';
          }
          _satellite.logger.info('source',source);
          _satellite.trackSearchSource(source);
        }
      });
    });

    //Right Rail
    const sidebarLawyerSearch = document.querySelector('.sidebarLawyerSearch');
    _satellite.logger.info('sidebarLawyerSearch',sidebarLawyerSearch);
    if (sidebarLawyerSearch) {
          sidebarLawyerSearch.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
            if (event.target.getAttribute('href') && event.target.getAttribute('href').includes('lawyers.findlaw.com')) {
              const goTo = event.target.getAttribute('href');
              _satellite.slowDown(event, goTo);
              _satellite.trackSearchSource("Link Module: Right Rail");
            }
          });
    }

    //Browse
    if (location.host + location.pathname == "lawyers.findlaw.com/") {
      const lawyerLinks = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/lawyer"]');
      _satellite.logger.info('lawyerLinks',lawyerLinks);
      lawyersLinks.forEach((link) => {
        link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          const goTo = this.getAttribute('href');
          _satellite.slowDown(e, goTo);
          let source = "";
          if (this.getAttribute("href").indexOf("/lawyer/statepractice/") > -1) {
            source = "Browse: Popular Cities";
          } else if (this.getAttribute("href").indexOf("/lawyer/state/") > -1) {
            source = "Browse: State";
          } else if (this.getAttribute("href").indexOf("/lawyer/statecounty/") > -1) {
            source = "Browse: Top Counties";
          } else if (this.getAttribute("href").indexOf("/lawyer/practice/") > -1) {
            source = "Browse: Legal Issue";
          }
          _satellite.logger.info('source',source);
          _satellite.trackSearchSource(source);
        });
      });
    }
    
    //data-search-location
    const linksWithSearchLocation = document.querySelectorAll('[data-search-location] a, a[data-search-location]');
    _satellite.logger.info('linksWithSearchLocation',linksWithSearchLocation);

        _satellite.logger.info('source',source);
        _satellite.trackSearchSource(source);
      });
    });
